## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: thermodynamics
**Analysis**: This task belongs to the domain of thermodynamics, specifically focusing on the relationship between stress, strain, and temperature. The physical behavior of materials under thermal conditions is a key aspect of this domain.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Rankine law: stress = c0 + 2*c1*strain + c2*strain**2 (elastic stress-strain relationship at high temperature)
- Hooke's law: stress = c0 + c1*strain (ideal elastic stress-strain relationship)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: strain = c0 + c1/T (thermal expansion strain-temperature relationship)
- Thermal stress: stress = c0 + c1*(T - T0) (thermal expansion induced stress at constant strain)
- Stress relaxation: stress = c0*exp(-c1*t/T) (decrease of stress with time at constant strain and temperature)
- Viscoelastic stress: stress = c0 + c1*exp(-c2*t/T) + c3*strain**c4 (non-ideal stress-strain relationship with time-dependent relaxation)
- Cumulative strain: strain = c0 + c1*stress + c2*stress**2 (non-linear cumulative strain under stress)
- Temperature-dependent material properties: stress = c0 + c1*strain + c2*strain**2/(T + c3) (non-linear stress-strain relationship with temperature-dependent parameters)
- Strain hardening: stress = c0 + c1*strain + c2*strain**2/(1 + c3*strain) (material hardening behavior with non-linear stress-strain relationship)
- Thermal expansion coefficient: strain = c0 + c1*(T - T0) (linear thermal expansion relationship)
- Modulus of elasticity: stress = c0 + c1*strain + c2*strain**2 (elastic stress-strain relationship with material-specific modulus)
- Creep rate: strain = c0 + c1*stress + c2*stress**2 (creep deformation under constant stress)
- Arrhenius equation for material properties: stress = c0 + c1*exp(-c2/kT) (temperature-dependent material properties with Arrhenius behavior)
- Thermal activation: stress = c0 + c1*exp(-c2/T) (non-linear thermal activation of material properties)
- Material degradation: stress = c0 + c1*strain + c2*strain**2 + c3*strain**3 (non-linear material degradation with time and strain)
- Time-dependent material properties: stress = c0 + c1*strain + c2*strain**2 + c3*exp(-c4*t/T) (time-dependent material properties with relaxation)
- Damage accumulation: strain = c0 + c1*stress + c2*stress**2 + c3*stress**3 (damage accumulation under cyclic loading)
- Diffusion-driven deformation: strain = c0 + c1*stress + c2*stress**2 + c3*exp(-c4*diffusion_coefficient*T) (diffusion-driven deformation under cyclic loading)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Temperature dependence → Arrhenius behavior f(T)*exp(-c0/kT), thermal expansion strain-T relationship, temperature-dependent material properties f(T,epsilon)
- Strain hardening behavior → Power-law relationship epsilon**(c0 + c1*stress), strain-hardening behavior with strain-dependent parameters
- Cumulative strain → Rational fraction epsilon/(1 + c0*stress), cumulative strain with saturation
- Thermal activation → Exponential function f(T)*exp(-c0/kT), thermal activation of material properties
- Material degradation → Rational fraction epsilon/(1 + c0*stress + c1*stress**2), material degradation with saturation
- Time-dependent material properties → Exponential decay f(t)*exp(-c0*t/T), time-dependent material properties with relaxation
- Damage accumulation → Rational fraction epsilon/(1 + c0*stress + c1*stress**2 + c2*stress**3), damage accumulation with saturation
- Diffusion-driven deformation → Exponential function f(diffusion_coefficient,T)*exp(-c0*kT), diffusion-driven deformation under cyclic loading
- Temperature-independent material properties → Linear or power-law relationship f(epsilon), temperature-independent material properties with non-linear relationship
